The scribe uses a high curl between \"Sancti\" and \"Brendani\" and above the punctuation mark between \"Brendani\" and \"Abbatis\". Further, the abbreviation marker for both \"at\" in \"Abbatis\" and \"er\" in \"Hybernia\" is given with the default combining vertical tilde. However, they may well be considered separate marks (perhaps the former a hook), especially given that they represent separate letter strings. There is also a mark like an acute accent above the \"a\" in \"Hybernia\". It is hard to tell whether it is brown or red ink, and, consequently whether is is a stray or meaningful mark.'><i class=\"fa fa-comment-o\"></i></tei-note></tei-ab> <tei-lg> <tei-l xml:id=\"bodllaudmisc108.3aa.1\"><tei-hi rend=\"h3 blue-ink\" class=\"h3 blue-ink\">S</tei-hi><tei-sg type=\"ln\"></tei-sg><tei-hi rend=\"touched-red\" class=\"touched-red\">E</tei-hi>int <tei-name type=\"person\" ref=\"#bioBrendan0001\"><tei-choice> <tei-orig>b<span class=\"dip\">&#42843;</span><span class=\"crit\">r</span>endan</tei-orig> <tei-reg>Brendan</tei-reg> </tei-choice></tei-name> &#254;e holi man<tei-pc><span class=\"dip\"> &#61793;
